#########################################################################
# 1100009 建立红军政治工作制度(CHC) 
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 1100009
	random = no
	country = CHC

	trigger = { incabinet = 51002 }

	name = "建立红军政治工作制度 "
	desc = "毛泽东同志领导建立红军政治工作制度。所谓政治工作制度，就 是党在军队中建立的进行政治工作的制度。它的内容是：团和相 当于团以上单位建立党委员会，设政治委员和政治机关；营和相 当于营的单位建立基层党委员会，设政治教导员；连和相当连的 单位建立党支部委员会，设政治指导员。红军政治工作制度的建 立，一方面保证了党对红军的绝对领导，另一方面也从实际上确 立了政治工作作为红军生命线的重要地位。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "sinuo_mao"

	date = { day = 10 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 1 month = december year = 1938 }

	action_a = {
		name = "建立 "
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 6030 }
		command = { type = gain_tech which = 6040 }
	}
}
#########################################################################
# 陕甘宁留守兵团的建立
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 61114
	random = no
	country = chc

	decision = { war = { country = JAP country = CHC } }

	decision_trigger = { 
		event = 1100026 # 红军改编
		owned = { province = 1271 data = CHC } # 延安
	}

			
	trigger = {
		event = 1100026 # 红军改编
		war = { country = JAP country = CHC }
		owned = { province = 1271 data = CHC } # 延安
	}

	name = "陕甘宁留守兵团的建立 "
	desc = "陕甘宁留守兵团为八路军的所属部队，1937年成立，司令员兼 政委为萧劲光，参谋长曹里怀，政治部主任莫文骅。"
	style = 2

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1937 }
	offset = 7
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1939 }

	action_a = {
		name = "保卫革命圣地安全！"
		command = { type = add_corps which = "G陕甘宁留守兵团 " value = land when = 76151 where = 1271 } #肖劲光
		command = { type = add_division which = "E警备第1旅 " value = infantry when = 47 where = anti_air }
		command = { type = add_division which = "E警备第2旅 " value = infantry when = 47 where = police }
		command = { type = add_division which = "A留守兵团教导旅 " value = bergsjaeger when = 24 where = engineer }
	}
}
#########################################################################
# 陕甘宁边区颁布《土地条例》
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 61305
	country = chc
	random = no

	trigger = {
		NOT = { ispuppet = CHC }
		war = { country = JAP country = CHC }
	}

	name = "陕甘宁边区颁布《土地条例》 "
	desc = "EVT_61305_DESC"
	style = 2
	picture = "tuditiaoli"

	date = { day = 3 month = april year = 1939 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 25 month = may year = 1939 }	

	action_a = {
		name = "土地问题是中国的根本问题 "
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { type = money value = -500 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = supplies value = 5 }
		command = { type = domestic which = democratic value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "维持旧有的土地政策不变 "
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = dissent value = 2 }
		command = { type = supplies value = 2000 }
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -1 }
	}
}

	}
}

# 1000110-114 陕甘宁边区政府事件组 (CHC、CHI) (by Civdemof)
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 1000110
	random = no
	country = chc

	decision = {
		war = { country = CHI country = JAP }
		war = { country = CHC country = JAP }
	        }

	decision_trigger = { 
		event = 90 #西安事变
		event = 91 #统一战线
	        }
			
	trigger = {
		event = 90 #西安事变
		event = 91 #统一战线
		war = { country = CHI country = JAP }
		war = { country = CHC country = JAP }
